## Section 002: Source Evidence Mapping Table
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed one local row hides that the row denotes three effectively distinct documents sharing a path, each guide names its own upstream bases, official platform documentation and engineering blogs for the first, Alex Xu's books and Kleppmann's Designing Data-Intensive Applications for the second and third, so provenance chains fork inside a single mapped file
- **supporting_reason:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the concatenation predates the corpus mapping, the queue mapped the file it found, and the evidence table inherits a one-row shape for what is evidentially a three-source bundle
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: treating the single row as a single authority overweights repetition, a pattern stated three times in the file may be one upstream claim copied thrice, or three independent formulations, and only reading the phrasings distinguishes these
- **assumptions_and_boundaries:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: apply the decision only within this boundary: provenance for the concatenated file's statements, the three external URLs stayed unretrieved and confer no current-fact authority
- **revision_decision:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to annotate the mapping with the three-guide split, each guide's self-declared upstream bases, and the second-hand nature of all engineering-blog and book citations inside it
- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 002 "Source Evidence Mapping Table", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that every technical claim in this theme is at least second-hand, the guides themselves are syntheses of blogs, books, and documentation, so the corpus row's local_corpus_sourced_fact label certifies only that the file says something, not that Netflix or Kleppmann said it, a two-hop chain the reuse discipline must preserve

## Section 004: Idiomatic Thesis Synthesis Statement
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 004 "Idiomatic Thesis Synthesis Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed generic corpus formulas stand where the source's actual thesis is stated in its own closing line, no pattern is universally correct, every pattern in all three guides ships with conditions, Use when, Avoid when, Anti-pattern, making the corpus a catalog of conditional rules rather than recommendations, and the skill it teaches is matching conditions, not memorizing solutions
- **supporting_reason:** Section 004 "Idiomatic Thesis Synthesis Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because distributed systems trade consistency, availability, latency, and cost against each other, so any unconditional pattern advice is wrong somewhere, and all three guides independently adopted condition-triplet formats to survive that reality
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 004 "Idiomatic Thesis Synthesis Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: extracting patterns without their conditions converts the corpus into cargo cult, the file itself catalogs the results, CQRS on simple CRUD, event sourcing without snapshots, push fanout for celebrity accounts, each an unconditioned pattern application

- **additional_insight_to_add:** Section 004 "Idiomatic Thesis Synthesis Statement", Question 01 on governing decision: add the consequence that the Use when, Avoid when, Anti-pattern triplet is itself the transferable pattern, three independent authors converged on shipping every rule with its activation conditions and its characteristic misuse, a documentation format that any reference corpus, including this evolution's own sections, can inherit

## Section 012: Local Corpus Hierarchy
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 012 "Local Corpus Hierarchy", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because concatenated guides were never reconciled by an editor, so small disagreements persist, differing canary percentages, differing snapshot cadence suggestions, and a consumer needs a precedence rule the file itself does not provide
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 012 "Local Corpus Hierarchy", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: citing whichever version was found first launders arbitrary choice as sourcing, the same query hitting a different guide would yield a different number with equal apparent authority

- **revision_decision:** Section 012 "Local Corpus Hierarchy", Question 01 on governing decision: revise the section to state the internal precedence rules, specificity for configuration, corroboration for principle, explicit both-versions citation when guides genuinely conflict

## Section 018: Workload Model
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed symbol-count boundary misprices this node's work, whose units are the sunk full read, roughly four hours of source at 3907 lines, per-question tri-guide searches, minutes each, per-audit seam checks plus stratified samples, well under an hour, and the standing drill investment, re-deriving worked designs at one to two hours each
- **supporting_reason:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because the source's size pushes every maintenance operation into the sampling regime, wholesale re-reads are special events, so the steady-state cost is dominated by per-question retrieval and periodic sampled audits
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 018 "Workload Model", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: under-budgeting the tri-guide search produces the partial-retrieval failure the source map warns about, single-hit answers from one guide when three treatments exist

## Section 021: Retry Backpressure Guidance
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?
- **current_section_observation:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the seed currently shows that the seed corpus-process bullets stand beside the source's definitive retry doctrine, exponential backoff computed as base times two to the attempt, full jitter randomizing the entire delay per AWS practice, retry budgets capping total volume across clients, retryable-error discrimination, 5xx and timeouts yes, 4xx except 429 no, and the stop conditions, open circuits and exhausted budgets end retrying
- **supporting_reason:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because correlated retries are load multipliers, so the doctrine's every element decorrelates or bounds them, jitter spreads timing, budgets cap volume, circuit state gates admission, and error discrimination stops futile attempts
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 021 "Retry Backpressure Guidance", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: the file names the failure twice as its own anti-pattern, unbounded retries in the headline list and no-jitter thundering herd in the retry entry, retry storms are the canonical self-inflicted outage

## Section 023: Performance Verification Method
### Question 01: What decision does this reference help make?

- **supporting_reason:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision matters because performance failures are usually arithmetic failures, designs that physically cannot meet their latency goals given the operations they chain, so the method front-loads the arithmetic before any optimization effort
- **counterargument_or_limit:** Section 023 "Performance Verification Method", Question 01 on governing decision: the decision must not conceal this limit: optimizing without a physical budget wastes effort on the wrong tier, shaving microseconds off cache lookups while a cross-region round trip dominates the budget by three orders of magnitude
